[30;1m6 | [0m[35mGQL provides a python script, called `gql-cli` which allows you to execute[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mGraphQL queries directly from the terminal.[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35mThis script supports http(s) or websockets protocols.[0m
[30;1m10 | [0m[35m[0m
